---
title: "E: Method http has died unexpectedly!"
date: 2009-08-20
forum: General Help
---

### Post by credobyte on 2009-08-20
Once my download speed exceeds 8Mb/s, I get an error: [COLOR=Red]E: Method http has died unexpectedly![/COLOR]
Update, packages .. whatever I try to install via terminal or Add/Remove, I get the same error. Is there a way to fix it ?

---

### Post by pedro_orange on 2009-08-20
Have you been adding lots of random repos?

Have you tried

```
sudo apt-get update
```

Which servers are the requests failing on?
Presumably you can reach these servers with ping/tracert?
Do you have IPv6 enabled? Might try disabling that and having another go.

---

### Post by credobyte on 2009-08-20
> **pedro_orange said:**
> Have you been adding lots of random repos?

Have you tried

```
sudo apt-get update
```Which servers are the requests failing on?
Presumably you can reach these servers with ping/tracert?
Do you have IPv6 enabled? Might try disabling that and having another go.

I'm talking about a fresh Ubuntu installation - first update fails 2-5 times, packages tend to give me this error as well. I've tried to change servers, however, both local servers ( Latvia ) gave me the same result .. IPv6 - how can I disable it ( no modem/router ) ?

---

### Post by pedro_orange on 2009-08-20
> **credobyte said:**
> I'm talking about a fresh Ubuntu installation - first update fails 2-5 times, packages tend to give me this error as well. I've tried to change servers, however, both local servers ( Latvia ) gave me the same result .. IPv6 - how can I disable it ( no modem/router ) ?

...Uhh what?

Post the hostnames of the servers you're trying to connect to?
Can you ping / tracert them?
Does your internet work? Can you get onto Google and do some web searches?
Also post your /etc/apt/sources.lst

Disabling IPv6: Depends on what Kernel you're using. Do the above stuff first, I doubt it's IPv6 issue - It may just be the servers are overloaded / slow.

---

### Post by Copernicus1234 on 2009-08-20
Try disabling ip6: [http://www.clububuntu.com/2009/01/how-to-disable-ipv6-in-ubuntu-810.html](http://www.clububuntu.com/2009/01/how-to-disable-ipv6-in-ubuntu-810.html)

Your problem sounds strange, so this is just a chance. If it doesnt solve the problem you can enable it again.

---

### Post by credobyte on 2009-08-20
I can ping them, I can use Google and this forum, I can download files from the net .. I can do whatever I want. I haven't had any connection problems while using download managers or torrents ( at full speed - 20Mb/s+ ). Only Aptitude seems to be a little buggy for me.

When I install Ubuntu, after logging in for the first time, I usually open Firefox, set appropriate configuration ( start page, downloads location, bookmarks ) and while surfing the net, I'm updating my PC.
It's strange when on every 20-30Mb ( 1/5 of an update ) I get this error :-|

Regarding server overload - I wouldn't be able to get such a speed in case if the statement above would be true.
